  * grade_story_104.txt (grade=4.6)
    While the story incorporates most assigned elements, they often feel forced rather than organic to the narrative. The brevity highlights rather than conceals the logical gaps in the plot. The central conflict lacks specificity—we never learn what the steward's actual mission entails or why the cameo matters beyond vague symbolism. The writing shows potential in its atmosphere but fails to develop a cohesive, compelling narrative with meaningful stakes.
